-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.加边框加流动渐变
local function C_4()
local script = G2L["4"];
	local frame = script.Parent
	
	-- 添加白色厚度1的UIStroke + 粉色渐变
	local s = Instance.new("UIStroke", frame)
	s.Thickness = 1
	s.Color = Color3.new(1,1,1)
	
	local g = Instance.new("UIGradient", s)
	g.Color = ColorSequence.new{
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0,   Color3.new(1,1,1)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.25,Color3.fromRGB(255,255,55)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,0)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.75,Color3.fromRGB(255,255,55)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1,   Color3.new(1,1,1))
	}
	
	-- 颜色流动（单向无限循环，3秒一圈）
	game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(
		g,
		TweenInfo.new(3, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.In, -1),
		{Offset = Vector2.new(1, 0)}
	):Play()
	
	-- 拖拽功能（手机+电脑通用）
	local dragging, dragStart, startPos
	local uis = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	
	local function update(input)
		if dragging then
			local delta = input.Position - dragStart
			frame.Position = UDim2.new(
				startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
				startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
			)
		end
	end
	
	frame.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
			dragging = true
			dragStart = input.Position
			startPos = frame.Position
	
			input.Changed:Connect(function()
				if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
					dragging = false
				end
			end)
		end
	end)
	
	frame.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
			update(input)
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_4);
-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.横分割线.流动渐变
local function C_6()
local script = G2L["6"];
	local gradient = script.Parent.UIGradient
	local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local tween = TweenService:Create(gradient, TweenInfo.new(3, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, -1, true), {Offset = Vector2.new(-1, 0)})
	tween:Play()
end;
task.spawn(C_6);

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.标题.文字随机变色
local function C_e()
local script = G2L["e"];
	local ts = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local label = script.Parent
	
	while true do
		local hue = tick() % 5 / 5          -- 5秒一圈彩虹，改大数字=更慢
		local color = Color3.fromHSV(hue, 1, 1)
	
		ts:Create(label, TweenInfo.new(1.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			TextColor3 = color
		}):Play()
	
		task.wait(1.2)
	end
end;
task.spawn(C_e);
-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.标题.文字设定

local script = G2L["f"];

local function C_11()
local script = G2L["11"];

	l.TextColor3=Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	
	--对齐方式
	l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
	
	--开启富文本

	--根据内容轴调整大小

	--开启自动换行
	l.TextWrapped = true
end;

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.关闭窗口.关闭
local function C_17()
local script = G2L["17"];
	-- 这个 LocalScript 直接放在 ImageButton 里面就行
	-- 结构：ScreenGui → Frame → ImageButton
	
	local button = script.Parent              -- 图片按钮
	local frame = button.Parent               -- Frame
	local screenGui = frame.Parent            -- ScreenGui
	
	local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
	
	-- 让所有 UI 元素渐隐（包括按钮自己）
	local function fadeOutAll()
		for _, obj in ipairs(screenGui:GetDescendants()) do
			if obj:IsA("GuiObject") then
				if obj:IsA("ImageButton") or obj:IsA("ImageLabel") then
					TweenService:Create(obj, tweenInfo, {ImageTransparency = 1}):Play()
				else
					TweenService:Create(obj, tweenInfo, {Transparency = 1}):Play()
				end
			end
		end
	end
	
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		fadeOutAll()                    -- 开始 3 秒渐隐
		task.delay(3, function()        -- 3秒后彻底关闭
			screenGui.Enabled = false   -- 隐藏 ScreenGui（最常用）
			-- 如果想永久删除，用下面这行代替：
			-- screenGui:Destroy()
		end)
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_17);

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.免费脚本.隐藏其他显示区
local function C_1b()
local script = G2L["1b"];
	-- LocalScript：直接放在“公告及活动”TextButton里面
	
	local button=script.Parent
	local frame=button.Parent
	
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		for _,sf in frame:GetChildren()do
			if sf:IsA("ScrollingFrame")then
				sf.Visible=sf.Name=="免费脚本显示区"
			end

	l.TextSize=16
	l.TextColor3=Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	
	--对齐方式
	l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
	
	--开启富文本
	l.RichText = true
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	l.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
	
	--开启自动换行
	l.TextWrapped = true
end;

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.玩家头像.显示玩家头像
local function C_42()
local script = G2L["42"];
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	local imageLabel = script.Parent
	
	local content, isReady = Players:GetUserThumbnailAsync(
		player.UserId,
		Enum.ThumbnailType.HeadShot,
		Enum.ThumbnailSize.Size420x420
	)
	
	imageLabel.Image = isReady and content or "rbxasset://textures/ui/GuiImagePlaceholder.png"
end;
task.spawn(C_42);

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.公告及活动显示区.滚动设定
local function C_47()
local script = G2L["47"];
	local sf=script.Parent
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	sf.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.None
	
	--滚动条粗细
	sf.ScrollBarThickness = 6
	
	--滚动条颜色
	sf.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 127)
	
	--自动计算画布大小
	sf.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
	
	--超出边缘自动裁切
	sf.ClipsDescendants = true
	
	--是否允许滚动
	sf.ScrollingEnabled = true
	
	--获取列表
	local listLayout = sf:WaitForChild("UIListLayout")
	
	--列表垂直排列
	listLayout.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Vertical
	
	--列表排列顺序
	listLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
	
	--列表行间距
	listLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 16)
	
	--不懂但有用
	local function updateCanvas()
		sf.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, listLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y)
	end
	
	-- 监听变化（实时更新，动态加元件完美）
	listLayout:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(updateCanvas)
	
	-- 初始更新（等布局计算完，避 Studio 延迟）
	task.spawn(function()
		task.wait()  -- 等 1 帧
		updateCanvas()
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_47);

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.免费脚本显示区.飞行.密钥验证
local function C_66()
local script = G2L["66"];
	-- LocalScript - 放在 ImageButton 里 (Xeon/Xeno 等注入器兼容)
	-- 使用 loadstring(game:HttpGet) 方式读取密钥（按你成功的方法）
	
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")
	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	
	local button = script.Parent
	
	-- 密钥地址（GitHub raw，目前内容为 robloxheikeji）
	local KEY_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/Key/refs/heads/main/FreeKey.txt"
	-- 最终要执行的脚本地址
	local SCRIPT_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/script/refs/heads/main/UniversalFly.txt"
	
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- 创建简洁的 UI
		local gui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
		gui.ResetOnSpawn = false
		gui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
	
		local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
		frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 340, 0, 190)
		frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -170, 0.5, -95)
		frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)          -- 纯白背景
		frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
		frame.Parent = gui
	
		local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 14)
		corner.Parent = frame
	
		-- 标题
		local title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		title.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 50)
		title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		title.Text = "Roblox黑科技脚本中心密钥系统"
		title.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)               -- 黑色
		title.TextSize = 20
		title.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold                -- 加粗
		title.TextWrapped = true
		title.Parent = frame
	
		-- 输入框（浅灰）
		local input = Instance.new("TextBox")
		input.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		input.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.32, 0)
		input.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)  -- 浅灰
		input.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		input.PlaceholderText = "请输入恁的密钥..."
		input.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 140, 140)
		input.Text = ""
		input.TextSize = 18
		input.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
		input.ClearTextOnFocus = false
		input.Parent = frame
	
		local inputCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		inputCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		inputCorner.Parent = input
	
		-- 提交按钮（浅灰）
		local submit = Instance.new("TextButton")
		submit.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		submit.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.58, 0)
		submit.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(235, 235, 235)  -- 浅灰
		submit.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		submit.Text = "俺要起飞"
		submit.TextSize = 18
		submit.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		submit.Parent = frame
	
		local submitCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		submitCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		submitCorner.Parent = submit
	
		-- 关闭按钮
		local close = Instance.new("TextButton")
		close.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
		close.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 6)
		close.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		close.Text = "×"
		close.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
		close.TextSize = 26
		close.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		close.Parent = frame
	
		close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			gui:Destroy()
		end)
	
		-- 提交逻辑（使用你成功的读取方式）
		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end
	
			local correctKey = tostring(result):gsub("%s+", ""):lower()  -- 清理
			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()
	
			if userInput == correctKey then
				gui:Destroy()
				local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
					loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
				end)
				if loadOk then
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})
				else
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "脚本加载失败",
						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_66);

	l.TextWrapped = true

		input.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		input.PlaceholderText = "请输入恁的密钥..."
		input.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 140, 140)
		input.Text = ""
		input.TextSize = 18
		input.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
		input.ClearTextOnFocus = false
		input.Parent = frame
	
		local inputCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		inputCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		inputCorner.Parent = input
	
		-- 提交按钮（浅灰）
		local submit = Instance.new("TextButton")
		submit.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		submit.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.58, 0)
		submit.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(235, 235, 235)  -- 浅灰
		submit.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		submit.Text = "俺要起飞"
		submit.TextSize = 18
		submit.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		submit.Parent = frame
	
		local submitCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		submitCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		submitCorner.Parent = submit
	
		-- 关闭按钮
		local close = Instance.new("TextButton")
		close.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
		close.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 6)
		close.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		close.Text = "×"
		close.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
		close.TextSize = 26
		close.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		close.Parent = frame
	
		close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			gui:Destroy()
		end)
	
		-- 提交逻辑（使用你成功的读取方式）
		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end
	
			local correctKey = tostring(result):gsub("%s+", ""):lower()  -- 清理
			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()
	
			if userInput == correctKey then
				gui:Destroy()
				local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
					loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
				end)
				if loadOk then
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})
				else
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "脚本加载失败",
						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.包月制脚本显示区.滚动设定
local function C_7f()
local script = G2L["7f"];
	local sf=script.Parent
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	sf.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.None
	
	--滚动条粗细
	sf.ScrollBarThickness = 6
	
	--滚动条颜色
	sf.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 127)
	
	--自动计算画布大小
	sf.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
	
	--超出边缘自动裁切
	sf.ClipsDescendants = true
	
	--是否允许滚动
	sf.ScrollingEnabled = true
	
	--获取列表
	local listLayout = sf:WaitForChild("UIListLayout")
	
	--列表垂直排列
	listLayout.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Vertical
	
	--列表排列顺序
	listLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
	
	--列表行间距
	listLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 16)
	
	--不懂但有用
	local function updateCanvas()
		sf.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, listLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y)
	end
	
	-- 监听变化（实时更新，动态加元件完美）
	listLayout:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(updateCanvas)
	
	-- 初始更新（等布局计算完，避 Studio 延迟）
	task.spawn(function()
		task.wait()  -- 等 1 帧
		updateCanvas()
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_7f);

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.包月制脚本显示区.伐木大亨2.密钥验证
local function C_84()
local script = G2L["84"];
	-- LocalScript - 放在 ImageButton 里 (Xeon/Xeno 等注入器兼容)
	-- 白名单模式：点击即检查用户名，无 UI 输入
	
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")
	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	
	local button = script.Parent
	
	-- 白名单地址
	local WHITELIST_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/Key/refs/heads/main/LumberTycoon2WhiteList.txt"
	-- 要执行的脚本地址
	local SCRIPT_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/script/refs/heads/main/LumberTycoon2.txt"
	
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- 立即显示正在比对提示（防止重复点击）
		StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
			Title = "包月制脚本白名单验证",
			Text = "正在检测恁在不在白名单，不要狂点以免卡顿...",
			Duration = 10
		})
	
		local success, result = pcall(function()
			return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. WHITELIST_URL .. '", true)')()
		end)
	
		if not success then
			StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
				Title = "无法连接服务器",
				Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题,导致恁连接不上白名单服务器",
				Duration = 8
			})
			return
		end
	
		-- 处理白名单内容
		local whitelistRaw = tostring(result):lower()
		local whitelist = {}
		for name in whitelistRaw:gmatch("[^,%s\r\n]+") do
			whitelist[name] = true
		end
	
		local playerNameLower = player.Name:lower()
	
		if whitelist[playerNameLower] then
			-- 成功：加载脚本
			local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
				loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
			end)
	
			if loadOk then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "白名单里有恁",
					Text = "对恁的身份核实完成，脚本已加载！",
					Duration = 6
				})
			else
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "脚本加载失败",
					Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致代码不可编译或载入失败",
					Duration = 8
				})
			end
		else
			-- 失败：提示信息（不踢人）
			StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
				Title = "白名单里没恁",
				Text = "请联系管理员购买，390751814微信QQ同号",
				Duration = 10
			})
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_84);

		for name in whitelistRaw:gmatch("[^,%s\r\n]+") do
			whitelist[name] = true
		end
	
		local playerNameLower = player.Name:lower()
	
		if whitelist[playerNameLower] then
			-- 成功：加载脚本
			local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
				loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
			end)
	
			if loadOk then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "白名单里有恁",
					Text = "对恁的身份核实完成，脚本已加载！",
					Duration = 6

			else
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "脚本加载失败",
					Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致代码不可编译或载入失败",
					Duration = 8
				})
			end
		else
			-- 失败：提示信息（不踢人）

local function C_93()
local script = G2L["93"];
	-- LocalScript - 放在 ImageButton 里 (Xeon/Xeno 等注入器兼容)
	-- 白名单模式：点击即检查用户名，无 UI 输入
	
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")
	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	
	local button = script.Parent
	
	-- 白名单地址
	local WHITELIST_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/Key/refs/heads/main/WarTycoonWhiteList.txt"
	-- 要执行的脚本地址
	local SCRIPT_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/script/refs/heads/main/WarTycoon.txt"
	
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- 立即显示正在比对提示（防止重复点击）
		StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
			Title = "包月制脚本白名单验证",
			Text = "正在检测恁在不在白名单，不要狂点以免卡顿...",
			Duration = 10
		})
	
		local success, result = pcall(function()
			return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. WHITELIST_URL .. '", true)')()
		end)
	
		if not success then
			StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
				Title = "无法连接服务器",
				Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题,导致恁连接不上白名单服务器",
				Duration = 8
			})
			return
		end
	
		-- 处理白名单内容
		local whitelistRaw = tostring(result):lower()
		local whitelist = {}
		for name in whitelistRaw:gmatch("[^,%s\r\n]+") do
			whitelist[name] = true
		end
	
		local playerNameLower = player.Name:lower()
	
		if whitelist[playerNameLower] then
			-- 成功：加载脚本
			local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
				loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
			end)
	
			if loadOk then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "白名单里有恁",
					Text = "对恁的身份核实完成，脚本已加载！",
					Duration = 6
				})
			else
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "脚本加载失败",
					Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致代码不可编译或载入失败",
					Duration = 8
				})
			end
		else
			-- 失败：提示信息（不踢人）
			StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
				Title = "白名单里没恁",
				Text = "请联系管理员购买，390751814微信QQ同号",
				Duration = 10
			})
		end
	end)
end;

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.买断制脚本显示区.滚动设定
local function C_a2()
local script = G2L["a2"];
	local sf=script.Parent
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	sf.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.None
	
	--滚动条粗细
	sf.ScrollBarThickness = 6
	
	--滚动条颜色
	sf.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 127)
	
	--自动计算画布大小
	sf.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
	
	--超出边缘自动裁切
	sf.ClipsDescendants = true
	
	--是否允许滚动
	sf.ScrollingEnabled = true
	
	--获取列表
	local listLayout = sf:WaitForChild("UIListLayout")
	
	--列表垂直排列
	listLayout.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Vertical
	
	--列表排列顺序
	listLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
	
	--列表行间距
	listLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 16)
	
	--不懂但有用
	local function updateCanvas()
		sf.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, listLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y)
	end
	
	-- 监听变化（实时更新，动态加元件完美）
	listLayout:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(updateCanvas)
	
	-- 初始更新（等布局计算完，避 Studio 延迟）
	task.spawn(function()
		task.wait()  -- 等 1 帧
		updateCanvas()
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_a2);

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.买断制脚本显示区.BloxFruit.密钥验证
local function C_a7()
local script = G2L["a7"];
	-- LocalScript - 放在 ImageButton 里 (Xeon/Xeno 等注入器兼容)
	-- 使用 loadstring(game:HttpGet) 方式读取密钥（按你成功的方法）
	
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")
	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	
	local button = script.Parent
	
	-- 密钥地址（GitHub raw，目前内容为 robloxheikeji）
	local KEY_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/Key/refs/heads/main/BloxFruitKey.txt"
	-- 最终要执行的脚本地址
	local SCRIPT_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/script/refs/heads/main/BloxFruit.txt"
	
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- 创建简洁的 UI
		local gui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
		gui.ResetOnSpawn = false
		gui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
	
		local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
		frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 340, 0, 190)
		frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -170, 0.5, -95)
		frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)          -- 纯白背景
		frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
		frame.Parent = gui
	
		local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 14)
		corner.Parent = frame
	
		-- 标题
		local title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		title.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 50)
		title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		title.Text = "Roblox黑科技脚本中心密钥系统"
		title.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)               -- 黑色
		title.TextSize = 20
		title.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold                -- 加粗
		title.TextWrapped = true
		title.Parent = frame
	
		-- 输入框（浅灰）
		local input = Instance.new("TextBox")
		input.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		input.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.32, 0)
		input.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)  -- 浅灰
		input.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		input.PlaceholderText = "请输入恁的密钥..."
		input.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 140, 140)
		input.Text = ""
		input.TextSize = 18
		input.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
		input.ClearTextOnFocus = false
		input.Parent = frame
	
		local inputCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		inputCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		inputCorner.Parent = input
	
		-- 提交按钮（浅灰）
		local submit = Instance.new("TextButton")
		submit.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		submit.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.58, 0)
		submit.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(235, 235, 235)  -- 浅灰
		submit.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		submit.Text = "俺要起飞"
		submit.TextSize = 18
		submit.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		submit.Parent = frame
	
		local submitCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		submitCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		submitCorner.Parent = submit
	
		-- 关闭按钮
		local close = Instance.new("TextButton")
		close.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
		close.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 6)
		close.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		close.Text = "×"
		close.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
		close.TextSize = 26
		close.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		close.Parent = frame
	
		close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			gui:Destroy()
		end)
	
		-- 提交逻辑（使用你成功的读取方式）
		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end
	
			local correctKey = tostring(result):gsub("%s+", ""):lower()  -- 清理
			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()
	
			if userInput == correctKey then
				gui:Destroy()
				local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
					loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
				end)
				if loadOk then
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})
				else
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "脚本加载失败",
						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_a7);

	-- 使用 loadstring(game:HttpGet) 方式读取密钥（按你成功的方法）
	
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")
	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	
	local button = script.Parent
	
	-- 密钥地址（GitHub raw，目前内容为 robloxheikeji）
	local KEY_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/Key/refs/heads/main/KinglegacyKey.txt"
	-- 最终要执行的脚本地址
	local SCRIPT_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/script/refs/heads/main/Kinglegacy.txt"
	
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- 创建简洁的 UI
		local gui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
		gui.ResetOnSpawn = false
		gui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
	
		local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
		frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 340, 0, 190)
		frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -170, 0.5, -95)
		frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)          -- 纯白背景
		frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
		frame.Parent = gui
	
		local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 14)
		corner.Parent = frame
	
		-- 标题
		local title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		title.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 50)
		title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		title.Text = "Roblox黑科技脚本中心密钥系统"
		title.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)               -- 黑色
		title.TextSize = 20
		title.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold                -- 加粗
		title.TextWrapped = true
		title.Parent = frame
	
		-- 输入框（浅灰）
		local input = Instance.new("TextBox")
		input.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		input.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.32, 0)
		input.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)  -- 浅灰
		input.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		input.PlaceholderText = "请输入恁的密钥..."
		input.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 140, 140)
		input.Text = ""
		input.TextSize = 18
		input.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
		input.ClearTextOnFocus = false
		input.Parent = frame
	
		local inputCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		inputCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		inputCorner.Parent = input
	
		-- 提交按钮（浅灰）
		local submit = Instance.new("TextButton")
		submit.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		submit.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.58, 0)
		submit.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(235, 235, 235)  -- 浅灰
		submit.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		submit.Text = "俺要起飞"
		submit.TextSize = 18
		submit.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		submit.Parent = frame
	
		local submitCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		submitCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		submitCorner.Parent = submit
	
		-- 关闭按钮
		local close = Instance.new("TextButton")
		close.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
		close.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 6)
		close.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		close.Text = "×"
		close.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
		close.TextSize = 26
		close.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		close.Parent = frame
	
		close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			gui:Destroy()
		end)
	
		-- 提交逻辑（使用你成功的读取方式）
		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end
	
			local correctKey = tostring(result):gsub("%s+", ""):lower()  -- 清理
			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()
	
			if userInput == correctKey then
				gui:Destroy()
				local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
					loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
				end)
				if loadOk then
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})
				else
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "脚本加载失败",
						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_ac);
-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.买断制脚本显示区.FishIt.脚本介绍.文字设定
local function C_af()
local script = G2L["af"];
	local l=script.Parent
	
	--使用Fredokaone字体，加粗，大小16，白色
	l.FontFace=Font.new("rbxasset://fonts/families/FredokaOne.json",Enum.FontWeight.Bold)
	l.TextSize=16
	l.TextColor3=Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	
	--对齐方式
	l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	
	--开启富文本
	l.RichText = true
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	l.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
	
	--开启自动换行
	l.TextWrapped = true
end;
task.spawn(C_af);

		submit.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		submit.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.58, 0)
		submit.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(235, 235, 235)  -- 浅灰
		submit.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		submit.Text = "俺要起飞"
		submit.TextSize = 18
		submit.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		submit.Parent = frame
	
		local submitCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		submitCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		submitCorner.Parent = submit
	
		-- 关闭按钮
		local close = Instance.new("TextButton")
		close.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
		close.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 6)
		close.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		close.Text = "×"
		close.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
		close.TextSize = 26
		close.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		close.Parent = frame
	
		close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			gui:Destroy()
		end)
	
		-- 提交逻辑（使用你成功的读取方式）
		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end
	
			local correctKey = tostring(result):gsub("%s+", ""):lower()  -- 清理
			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()
	
			if userInput == correctKey then
				gui:Destroy()
				local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
					loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
				end)
				if loadOk then
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})
				else
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "脚本加载失败",
						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.买断制脚本显示区.被遗弃.脚本介绍.文字设定
local function C_be()
local script = G2L["be"];
	local l=script.Parent
	
	--使用Fredokaone字体，加粗，大小16，白色
	l.FontFace=Font.new("rbxasset://fonts/families/FredokaOne.json",Enum.FontWeight.Bold)
	l.TextSize=16
	l.TextColor3=Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	
	--对齐方式
	l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	
	--开启富文本
	l.RichText = true
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	l.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
	
	--开启自动换行
	l.TextWrapped = true
end;
task.spawn(C_be);

				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)

-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.买断制脚本显示区.弹钢琴.脚本介绍.文字设定
local function C_cd()
local script = G2L["cd"];
	local l=script.Parent
	
	--使用Fredokaone字体，加粗，大小16，白色
	l.FontFace=Font.new("rbxasset://fonts/families/FredokaOne.json",Enum.FontWeight.Bold)
	l.TextSize=16
	l.TextColor3=Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	
	--对齐方式
	l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	
	--开启富文本
	l.RichText = true
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	l.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
	
	--开启自动换行
	l.TextWrapped = true
end;
task.spawn(C_cd);
-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.买断制脚本显示区.弹钢琴.密钥验证
local function C_cf()
local script = G2L["cf"];
	-- LocalScript - 放在 ImageButton 里 (Xeon/Xeno 等注入器兼容)
	-- 使用 loadstring(game:HttpGet) 方式读取密钥（按你成功的方法）
	
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")
	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	
	local button = script.Parent
	
	-- 密钥地址（GitHub raw，目前内容为 robloxheikeji）
	local KEY_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/Key/refs/heads/main/UniversalPianoKey.txt"
	-- 最终要执行的脚本地址
	local SCRIPT_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/script/refs/heads/main/UniversalPiano.txt"
	
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- 创建简洁的 UI
		local gui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
		gui.ResetOnSpawn = false
		gui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
	
		local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
		frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 340, 0, 190)
		frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -170, 0.5, -95)
		frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)          -- 纯白背景
		frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
		frame.Parent = gui
	
		local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 14)
		corner.Parent = frame
	
		-- 标题
		local title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		title.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 50)
		title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		title.Text = "Roblox黑科技脚本中心密钥系统"
		title.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)               -- 黑色
		title.TextSize = 20
		title.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold                -- 加粗
		title.TextWrapped = true
		title.Parent = frame
	
		-- 输入框（浅灰）
		local input = Instance.new("TextBox")
		input.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		input.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.32, 0)
		input.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)  -- 浅灰
		input.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		input.PlaceholderText = "请输入恁的密钥..."
		input.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 140, 140)
		input.Text = ""
		input.TextSize = 18
		input.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
		input.ClearTextOnFocus = false
		input.Parent = frame
	
		local inputCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		inputCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		inputCorner.Parent = input
	
		-- 提交按钮（浅灰）
		local submit = Instance.new("TextButton")
		submit.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		submit.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.58, 0)
		submit.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(235, 235, 235)  -- 浅灰
		submit.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		submit.Text = "俺要起飞"
		submit.TextSize = 18
		submit.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		submit.Parent = frame
	
		local submitCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		submitCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		submitCorner.Parent = submit
	
		-- 关闭按钮
		local close = Instance.new("TextButton")
		close.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
		close.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 6)
		close.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		close.Text = "×"
		close.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
		close.TextSize = 26
		close.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		close.Parent = frame
	
		close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			gui:Destroy()
		end)
	
		-- 提交逻辑（使用你成功的读取方式）
		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end
	
			local correctKey = tostring(result):gsub("%s+", ""):lower()  -- 清理
			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()
	
			if userInput == correctKey then
				gui:Destroy()
				local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
					loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
				end)
				if loadOk then
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})
				else
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "脚本加载失败",
						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_cf);

		frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)          -- 纯白背景
		frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
		frame.Parent = gui
	
		local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 14)
		corner.Parent = frame
	
		-- 标题
		local title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		title.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 50)
		title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		title.Text = "Roblox黑科技脚本中心密钥系统"
		title.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)               -- 黑色
		title.TextSize = 20
		title.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold                -- 加粗
		title.TextWrapped = true
		title.Parent = frame
	
		-- 输入框（浅灰）
		local input = Instance.new("TextBox")
		input.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		input.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.32, 0)
		input.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)  -- 浅灰
		input.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		input.PlaceholderText = "请输入恁的密钥..."
		input.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 140, 140)
		input.Text = ""
		input.TextSize = 18
		input.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
		input.ClearTextOnFocus = false
		input.Parent = frame
	
		local inputCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		inputCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		inputCorner.Parent = input
	
		-- 提交按钮（浅灰）
		local submit = Instance.new("TextButton")
		submit.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		submit.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.58, 0)
		submit.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(235, 235, 235)  -- 浅灰
		submit.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		submit.Text = "俺要起飞"
		submit.TextSize = 18
		submit.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		submit.Parent = frame
	
		local submitCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		submitCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		submitCorner.Parent = submit
	
		-- 关闭按钮
		local close = Instance.new("TextButton")
		close.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
		close.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 6)
		close.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		close.Text = "×"
		close.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
		close.TextSize = 26
		close.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		close.Parent = frame
	
		close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			gui:Destroy()
		end)
	
		-- 提交逻辑（使用你成功的读取方式）
		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end
	
			local correctKey = tostring(result):gsub("%s+", ""):lower()  -- 清理
			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()
	
			if userInput == correctKey then
				gui:Destroy()
				local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
					loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
				end)
				if loadOk then
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})
				else
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "脚本加载失败",
						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_de);
-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.买断制脚本显示区.最强战场.脚本介绍.文字设定
local function C_e1()
local script = G2L["e1"];
	local l=script.Parent
	
	--使用Fredokaone字体，加粗，大小16，白色
	l.FontFace=Font.new("rbxasset://fonts/families/FredokaOne.json",Enum.FontWeight.Bold)
	l.TextSize=16
	l.TextColor3=Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	
	--对齐方式
	l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	
	--开启富文本
	l.RichText = true
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	l.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
	
	--开启自动换行
	l.TextWrapped = true
end;
task.spawn(C_e1);

local function C_e3()

	local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")

		-- 创建简洁的 UI

		gui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")

		frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -170, 0.5, -95)

		close.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
		close.TextSize = 26
		close.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		close.Parent = frame
	
		close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			gui:Destroy()
		end)
	
		-- 提交逻辑（使用你成功的读取方式）
		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end
	
			local correctKey = tostring(result):gsub("%s+", ""):lower()  -- 清理
			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()
	
			if userInput == correctKey then
				gui:Destroy()
				local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
					loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
				end)
				if loadOk then
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})
				else
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "脚本加载失败",
						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;

	l.FontFace=Font.new("rbxasset://fonts/families/FredokaOne.json",Enum.FontWeight.Bold)
	l.TextSize=16

	--对齐方式
	l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	
	--开启富文本
	l.RichText = true
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	l.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
	
	--开启自动换行
	l.TextWrapped = true
end;
task.spawn(C_ff);
-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.买断制脚本显示区.刀刃球.密钥验证
local function C_101()
local script = G2L["101"];
	-- LocalScript - 放在 ImageButton 里 (Xeon/Xeno 等注入器兼容)
	-- 使用 loadstring(game:HttpGet) 方式读取密钥（按你成功的方法）
	
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")
	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	
	local button = script.Parent
	
	-- 密钥地址（GitHub raw，目前内容为 robloxheikeji）
	local KEY_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/Key/refs/heads/main/BladeBallKey.txt"
	-- 最终要执行的脚本地址
	local SCRIPT_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RBMHUB/script/refs/heads/main/BladeBall.txt"
	
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		-- 创建简洁的 UI
		local gui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
		gui.ResetOnSpawn = false
		gui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
	
		local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
		frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 340, 0, 190)
		frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -170, 0.5, -95)
		frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)          -- 纯白背景
		frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
		frame.Parent = gui
	
		local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 14)
		corner.Parent = frame
	
		-- 标题
		local title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		title.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 50)
		title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		title.Text = "Roblox黑科技脚本中心密钥系统"
		title.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)               -- 黑色
		title.TextSize = 20
		title.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold                -- 加粗
		title.TextWrapped = true
		title.Parent = frame
	
		-- 输入框（浅灰）
		local input = Instance.new("TextBox")
		input.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		input.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.32, 0)
		input.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)  -- 浅灰
		input.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		input.PlaceholderText = "请输入恁的密钥..."
		input.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 140, 140)
		input.Text = ""
		input.TextSize = 18
		input.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
		input.ClearTextOnFocus = false
		input.Parent = frame
	
		local inputCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		inputCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		inputCorner.Parent = input
	
		-- 提交按钮（浅灰）
		local submit = Instance.new("TextButton")
		submit.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		submit.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.58, 0)
		submit.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(235, 235, 235)  -- 浅灰
		submit.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		submit.Text = "俺要起飞"
		submit.TextSize = 18
		submit.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		submit.Parent = frame
	
		local submitCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		submitCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		submitCorner.Parent = submit
	
		-- 关闭按钮
		local close = Instance.new("TextButton")
		close.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
		close.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 6)
		close.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		close.Text = "×"
		close.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
		close.TextSize = 26
		close.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		close.Parent = frame
	
		close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			gui:Destroy()
		end)
	
		-- 提交逻辑（使用你成功的读取方式）
		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end
	
			local correctKey = tostring(result):gsub("%s+", ""):lower()  -- 清理
			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()
	
			if userInput == correctKey then
				gui:Destroy()
				local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
					loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
				end)
				if loadOk then
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})
				else
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "脚本加载失败",
						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_101);

		frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -170, 0.5, -95)
		frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)          -- 纯白背景
		frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
		frame.Parent = gui
	
		local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 14)
		corner.Parent = frame
	
		-- 标题
		local title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		title.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 50)
		title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		title.Text = "Roblox黑科技脚本中心密钥系统"
		title.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)               -- 黑色
		title.TextSize = 20
		title.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold                -- 加粗
		title.TextWrapped = true
		title.Parent = frame
	
		-- 输入框（浅灰）
		local input = Instance.new("TextBox")
		input.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		input.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.32, 0)
		input.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)  -- 浅灰
		input.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		input.PlaceholderText = "请输入恁的密钥..."
		input.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 140, 140)
		input.Text = ""
		input.TextSize = 18
		input.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
		input.ClearTextOnFocus = false
		input.Parent = frame
	
		local inputCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		inputCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		inputCorner.Parent = input
	
		-- 提交按钮（浅灰）
		local submit = Instance.new("TextButton")
		submit.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0, 42)
		submit.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.58, 0)
		submit.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(235, 235, 235)  -- 浅灰
		submit.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
		submit.Text = "俺要起飞"
		submit.TextSize = 18
		submit.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		submit.Parent = frame
	
		local submitCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		submitCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
		submitCorner.Parent = submit
	
		-- 关闭按钮
		local close = Instance.new("TextButton")
		close.Size = UDim2.new(0, 34, 0, 34)
		close.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 6)
		close.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		close.Text = "×"
		close.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
		close.TextSize = 26
		close.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
		close.Parent = frame
	
		close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			gui:Destroy()
		end)
	
		-- 提交逻辑（使用你成功的读取方式）
		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end
	
			local correctKey = tostring(result):gsub("%s+", ""):lower()  -- 清理
			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()
	
			if userInput == correctKey then
				gui:Destroy()
				local loadOk, err = pcall(function()
					loadstring(game:HttpGet(SCRIPT_URL, true))()
				end)
				if loadOk then
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})
				else
					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "脚本加载失败",
						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_114);

local function C_117()
local script = G2L["117"];
	local l=script.Parent
	
	--使用Fredokaone字体，加粗，大小16，白色
	l.FontFace=Font.new("rbxasset://fonts/families/FredokaOne.json",Enum.FontWeight.Bold)
	l.TextSize=16
	l.TextColor3=Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	
	--对齐方式
	l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	
	--开启富文本
	l.RichText = true
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	l.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
	
	--开启自动换行
	l.TextWrapped = true
end;

			gui:Destroy()
		end)

		local function checkKey()
			local success, result = pcall(function()
				return loadstring('return game:HttpGet("' .. KEY_URL .. '", true)')()
			end)
	
			if not success then
				StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
					Title = "无法连接服务器",
					Text = "大概率是恁的网络或者加速器VPN的问题，导致恁提交了空密钥",
					Duration = 6
				})
				return
			end

			local userInput = input.Text:gsub("%s+", ""):lower()

				end)

					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
						Title = "密钥已嵌入",
						Text = "恁的脚本加载成功！",
						Duration = 5
					})

					StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {

						Text = "大概率是恁的注入器或加速器VPN的问题，导致脚本不可编译或载入失败",
						Duration = 6
					})
				end
			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)

			end
		end)
	end)

		title.TextSize = 20

			else
				-- 修改为：输入错误 → 直接踢出玩家
				player:Kick("恁的密钥不对，所以踢恁下线，请核实密钥或联系管理员获取，390751814微信QQ同号")
			end
		end
	
		-- 点击按钮 & 回车都可提交
		submit.MouseButton1Click:Connect(checkKey)
		input.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
			if enterPressed then
				checkKey()
			end
		end)
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_136);
-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.Frame.最小化窗口.文字设定
local function C_138()
local script = G2L["138"];
	local l=script.Parent
	
	--使用Fredokaone字体，加粗，大小16，白色
	l.FontFace=Font.new("rbxasset://fonts/families/FredokaOne.json",Enum.FontWeight.Bold)
	l.TextSize=16
	l.TextColor3=Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	
	--对齐方式
	l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
	
	--开启富文本
	l.RichText = true
	
	--根据内容轴调整大小
	l.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
	
	--开启自动换行
	l.TextWrapped = true
end;
task.spawn(C_138);
-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.展开窗口.拖动
local function C_13b()
local script = G2L["13b"];
	local button = script.Parent
	local UIS = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	
	local dragging, dragStart, startPos
	
	button.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
		if (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or 
			input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) and not dragging then
			dragging = true
			dragStart = input.Position
			startPos = button.Position
		end
	end)
	
	button.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
		if dragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or 
			input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
			local delta = input.Position - dragStart
			button.Position = UDim2.new(
				startPos.X.Scale,
				startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
				startPos.Y.Scale,
				startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
			)
		end
	end)
	
	button.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or 
			input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
			dragging = false
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_13b);
-- StarterGui.ScreenGui.最小化窗口
local function C_13c()
local script = G2L["13c"];
	-- LocalScript 放在 ScreenGui 底下（推荐位置）
	
	local screenGui = script.Parent  -- 当前 ScreenGui
	
	-- 取得物件（用 WaitForChild 确保物件已加载）
	local mainFrame   = screenGui:WaitForChild("Frame")                -- 你的主 Frame
	local minButton   = mainFrame:WaitForChild("最小化窗口")           -- TextButton（最小化）
	local expandButton = screenGui:WaitForChild("展开窗口")            -- ImageButton（展开）
	
	-- 1. 点击最小化按钮：隐藏 Frame + 显示展开按钮
	minButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		mainFrame.Visible = false
		expandButton.Visible = true
	end)
	
	-- 2. 点击展开按钮：显示 Frame + 隐藏展开按钮
	expandButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		mainFrame.Visible = true
		expandButton.Visible = false
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_13c);

return G2L["1"], require;
